<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 突破Dagan等人（2024）之前工作中校准误差的T^{2/3}下界，进一步提高在线二元序贯校准问题的性能。

Method: 将SPR-Calibration程序与外部Blackwell风格校正层相结合。SPR-Calibration控制相对于替代条件均值估计序列的校准误差，校正层则控制使用这些替代值近似真实结果时产生的额外误差。通过二次势参数论证和SPR-Calibration预测器的稀疏性来控制残差。

Result: 实现了期望校准误差O(T^{2/3-ε})，其中ε>0为某常数，优于经典的T^{2/3}界。

Abstract: We study the online binary sequential calibration problem. A recent breakthrough by \citet{dagan2024breaking} overcomes the classical \(T^{2/3}\) barrier for calibration error. Building on this result, we present an efficient randomized forecaster that achieves an expected calibration error \(O(T^{2/3-\varepsilon})\) for some constant \(\varepsilon>0\).
  Our forecaster combines the \textsc{SPR-Calibration} procedure \citep{dagan2024breaking} with an outer Blackwell-style correction layer. The \textsc{SPR-Calibration} procedure controls calibration with respect to a surrogate sequence of conditional-mean estimates, while the correction layer controls the additional error incurred when these surrogates are used to approximate the true outcomes. The analysis decomposes the total calibration error into the surrogate calibration error and the residual discrepancy between the surrogate sequence and the true outcomes. The former is bounded by the \textsc{SPR-Calibration} guarantee in \citet{dagan2024breaking}, and the latter is controlled using a quadratic potential argument together with the sparsity of the \textsc{SPR-Calibration} forecaster.

### [284] [The Spectrum Is Not Enough: When Context Helps Time-Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13006)
*Mert Onur Cakiroglu,Mehmet Dalkilic,Hasan Kurban*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出，基于功率谱的可预测性指数（如谱残差、熵等）回答的是"序列本身的可预测性"，而实践者常误用它们来回答"添加上下文（长回溯、检索增强、预训练模型）能否提升预测效果"。作者通过相位随机化构造代理对（相同谱、相同边缘分布但相位随机化），证明谱指数无法区分原始序列与随机化序列，而检索和基础模型提供的超二阶价值会在代理对上崩溃。作者提出标签无关的诊断指标——覆盖亏缺（coverage deficit），其核心项通过模拟预测与线性预测的增益衡量超谱结构。实验验证：基于窗口键的检索价值在代理对上中位数从+33%跌至-35%，基础模型的价值中超出线性部分崩溃，而更长线性窗口的价值保持不变。结论是：谱指数只能回答"二阶可预测性"，无法用于判断上下文是否有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实践者常用谱指数（如谱残差、熵等）来衡量一个序列是否可预测，但误用它们来回答"添加上下文（长回溯、检索增强、预训练模型）是否有助于提升预测"。这两个问题本质不同，谱指数仅捕捉二阶统计特性（功率谱），而上下文价值依赖高阶结构和相位信息。作者旨在指出这一混淆，并给出理论分析和实用诊断。

Method: 1) 通过相位随机化构造代理对（surrogate pairs），固定功率谱和边缘分布但随机化相位，使得相位随机化序列渐近高斯化。2) 证明任何基于功率谱的指数在代理对上不变（不可区分原始与随机化序列），而检索/预训练模型的价值会在代理对上崩溃。3) 提出覆盖亏缺（coverage deficit），其核心项衡量模拟预测与线性预测的增益，即超谱结构。4) 在7个基准数据集上验证：窗口键检索的中位数收益从+33%降至-35%（p<10^{-40}）；基础模型的价值分裂为幸存二阶部分和崩溃的超线性部分；长线性窗口价值不变。

Result: 1) 窗口键检索在代理对上中位数收益从+33%跌至-35%（p<10^{-40}），所有谱指数不变。2) 基础模型（如LLM类时间序列模型）的价值分裂：二阶部分幸存，超线性部分崩溃。3) 更长线性窗口的价值在代理对上不变。4) 留一数据集验证：超谱结构项能预测超谱价值的符号，而谱指数则不能。

Conclusion: 谱指数只反映序列的二阶可预测性，不能用于判断上下文（检索、预训练模型等）是否有效。覆盖亏缺是更好的标签无关诊断指标，能区分二阶价值与超谱结构价值。实践者在部署决策时应使用覆盖亏缺而非谱指数。

Abstract: A growing family of indices scores how predictable a series is from its spectrum. Practitioners increasingly read these scores as answering a different question: whether \emph{adding context}, a longer lookback, a retrieval plug-in, or a pretrained model, will help. These are not the same question. The value of context is a property of the operating point, not of the series. Any index built from the power spectrum is invariant under phase randomization, whereas the beyond-second-order value that retrieval and foundation models supply is not, because a phase-randomized series is asymptotically Gaussian. We state this as an impossibility result and isolate it with surrogate pairs that fix the spectrum and the marginal by construction. We then give a label-free, configuration-level diagnostic, the coverage deficit, whose principal term measures beyond-spectrum structure as the gain of analog over linear prediction. On seven benchmarks the prediction holds: window-keyed retrieval's value collapses across surrogate pairs (ECL median $+33\%\!\to\!-35\%$, $p{<}10^{-40}$) while every spectral index stays frozen; a foundation model's value splits into a surviving second-order part and a small beyond-linear margin that collapses; a longer linear window's value survives. Leave-one-dataset-out, the structure term predicts the sign of beyond-spectrum value where the spectral indices trail it, and the reverse holds for the second-order mechanism. We introduce no new forecaster; the contribution is the distinction, a controlled comparison, and a diagnostic for the deployment decision. Code: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/SINE.

</details>

We present TerraZero, a procedural driving simulator and self-play training stack. A configurable C engine runs simulation on the CPU and policy inference on the GPU over a zero-copy path, sustaining 1.3M agent-steps per second on a single server-grade GPU, far faster than existing object-level simulators, while keeping fidelity lighter single-agent systems omit: heterogeneous agents, multiple dynamics models, and full traffic-rule enforcement. TerraZero treats logged data only as a source of real-world map geometry, populating each map with randomized rule-based road users and signal controllers and randomizing agent dynamics, rewards, and sizes per episode, so a map yields an unbounded set of scenarios. Every reported policy trains from scratch by reinforcement learning alone on a compute-efficient self-play recipe across GPUs, with zero human demonstrations and no fallback planner at inference. Policies generalize zero-shot across cities and datasets, including emergent left-hand-traffic driving without explicit supervision. ### [286] [The Seriality Gap in Video Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13031)
*Jorge Diaz Chao,Konpat Preechakul,Yuxi Liu,Yutong Bai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 视频扩散模型在预测多球碰撞的因果链时表现随链长增加而下降，而在无交互的单球控制实验中无明显退化。研究发现这是由于序列性差距——任务需要递增的串行计算，但扩散模型的去噪循环无法提供可扩展的串行处理能力。作者还从理论上证明了去噪步数不增加超过骨干网络的串行计算量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索标准双向视频扩散模型在处理需要串行推理（如多球碰撞的因果链预测）时的性能瓶颈，并揭示其结构性的计算限制。

Method: 通过多球硬球动力学实验，对比多球（含因果依赖）与单球（无交互）视频预测任务，进行干预研究（如自回归生成、块生成、增加深度），并给出理论证明。

Result: 视频扩散模型在因果链增长时性能明显下降；单球对照组无此退化；增加串行计算（自回归/块生成、加深网络）可改善性能；理论证明去噪步数不增加串行计算量。

Conclusion: 存在序列性差距，视频扩散模型的结构性障碍使其难以胜任需要可扩展串行推理的任务，为未来模型设计提供重要方向。

Abstract: When one ball strikes another, then another, video models should predict the consequences of each bounce. In controlled experiments on multi-ball hard-sphere dynamics, we find that the performance of standard bidirectional video diffusion degrades as the causal chain lengthens, even when provided more denoising steps. In a length-matched single-ball control, where ball-ball interactions are absent, the degradation largely disappears, isolating dependent-event structure rather than video length as the cause. Across intervention studies, methods that increase effective serial computation improve performance disproportionately, including autoregressive/blockwise generation and architectural depth. We identify this pattern as the seriality gap: a mismatch between tasks requiring growing serial computation and video diffusion models whose denoising loop does not provide scalable serial compute. We then prove that, for deterministic video prediction, denoising steps do not add serial computation beyond the backbone, indicating a structural obstacle for video diffusion on serial reasoning and simulation tasks.

### [287] [Bounded Analog Complexity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12234)
*Ho-Lin Chen,Xiang Huang*

Main category: cs.CC

TL;DR: 本文提出有界模拟复杂度理论，通过“有界替代编译”框架将无界多项式ODE系统转化为有界系统，同时保持计算极限和时间精度保证。在有界GPAC模型下，展示了精细的时间复杂度构造，并证明了有界GPAC在指数运算下的封闭性以及GPAC到CRN编译流水线的时间复杂度保持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模拟复杂度理论（基于GPAC和多项式ODE）允许无界状态变量，这在化学反应网络等实验室规模模拟计算机中物理上不现实。因此需要发展一种所有状态变量保持在紧致区间内的有界模拟复杂度理论。

Method: 提出有界替代编译框架，将无界多项式ODE系统转化为有界系统；通过低通滤波器分析读出模块，证明GPAC到CRN的编译流水线保持时间复杂度类别；构造具体示例展示精细有界时间复杂度。

Result: 证明了编译后系统的物理时间在原始系统的弧长和时间的多项式范围内；展示了可调多项式族、Lambert-W系统（Θ(r log r)时间精度）、迭代对数塔等构造；证明了有界GPAC在指数运算下封闭，且GPAC-to-CRN编译流水线保持时间复杂度类别。

Conclusion: 建立了有界模拟复杂度理论，为物理可实现模拟计算机提供了更现实的理论基础，并展示了有界系统仍能实现丰富的复杂度层次。

Abstract: Current analog complexity theory, built on the General-Purpose Analog Computer (GPAC) model and polynomial ODEs, allows unbounded state variables -- an assumption that is physically unrealistic for chemical reaction networks and other laboratory-scale analog computers. We develop a bounded analog complexity theory in which all state variables remain in compact intervals and physical time (wall-clock time) is the only diverging resource.
  Our main technical contribution is bounded surrogate compilation, a compilation framework that transforms unbounded polynomial ODE systems into bounded ones while preserving computational limits and time-to-precision guarantees. We prove that if a system is compiled into a bounded system through our algorithm, the wall-clock time of the compiled system is polynomial in the arc length and physical time of the original system.
  We exhibit concrete constructions demonstrating fine-grained bounded time complexity -- a tunable polynomial-degree family, a Lambert-$W$-based system achieving $Θ(r\log r)$ time-to-precision (where $r$ is the desired precision parameter, in nats: $|x(t)-α|<e^{-r}$), and an iterated-logarithm tower realizing arbitrarily high complexity classes -- all for the task of computing the constant 1. We show that bounded GPACs are closed under exponentiation ($α^β$) with time complexity equal to the harder input, and that the full GPAC-to-CRN compilation pipeline preserves time complexity class via a low-pass filter analysis of readout modules.

</details>


### [288] [ETH-Hardness of Learning Monotone Circuits and Approximating Their Size](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12331)
*Bruno Cavalar,Susanna F. de Rezende,Matthew Gray,Rahul Santhanam*

Main category: cs.CC

TL;DR: 本文证明了在随机化指数时间假说（rETH）下，单调公式的PAC学习和单调电路规模的近似都是困难的，需要接近拟多项式时间。结果通过将证明与通信复杂性中的lifting论证应用于单调学习问题得到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究单调学习与单调电路规模近似的计算复杂性下限，填补在该领域缺乏强下界结果的空白。

Method: 基于rETH假设，利用lifting论证将证明与通信复杂性的硬度结果转移到单调学习问题上，借鉴了Atserias和Müller关于Resolution证明自动化难度的经典工作。

Result: 1) PAC学习大小为n的单调公式需要n^{Ω(log n)}时间；2) 单调电路规模的近似也需要m^{Ω(log m)}时间。

Conclusion: 在rETH下，单调学习和单调电路规模近似本质上都是拟多项式时间难解的。

Abstract: We show the following hardness results for monotone learning and approximation of monotone circuit size:
  1. Under the Randomised Exponential-Time Hypothesis (rETH), it requires time $n^{Ω(\log n)}$ to PAC-learn monotone formulas with $n$ input bits and size $s(n) = n$ by monotone circuits of size $n^{(\log n)^{1-ε}}$, for every $ε> 0$.
  2. Under the Randomised Exponential-Time Hypothesis (rETH), for any $δ> 0$, there is a polynomially bounded function $m$ such that $m^{1-δ}$-multiplicatively approximating the minimum monotone circuit size of a monotone function consistent with a sequence of $m(n)$ labelled examples $\{(x_i, b_i)\}$ over $n$-bit inputs requires time $m^{Ω(\log(m))}$.
  Our results are shown by a novel application of lifting arguments in proof and communication complexity to hardness of monotone learning, by building on the seminal result of Atserias and Müller (J. ACM, 2020) on hardness of automating Resolution proofs.

### [289] [Degree Lower Bounds for Torus Polynomials and $MAJORITY$ vs $ACC^0$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12346)
*Vaibhav Krishan,Sundar Vishwanathan*

Main category: cs.CC

TL;DR: 本文通过将MAJORITY不属于ACC^0的猜想归约到线性规划可行解问题，并利用对偶多项式方法找到了大量线性规划的可行解，为证明该猜想提供了增量式进展的新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MAJORITY是否属于ACC^0是计算复杂性理论中的一个核心猜想，但长期以来缺乏有效的证明方法。本文致力于通过环面多项式逼近的方法来攻克这一猜想。

Method: 将猜想归约为无限族线性规划的可行解问题，采用对偶多项式方法，通过增量式地求解线性规划来逐步逼近目标。首先找到了大量线性规划的可行解，仅剩有限集待处理。

Result: 找到了大量线性规划的可行解，将无限问题简化为有限问题；同时证明了AND函数的逼近下界以及对称多项式逼近的下界。

Conclusion: 该工作为证明MAJORITY不属于ACC^0提供了一个新的、可增量推进的研究框架，验证了方法的有效性。

Abstract: The class $ACC^0$ consists of Boolean functions that can be computed by constant-depth circuits of polynomial size with $AND, NOT$ and $MOD_m$ gates, where $m$ is a natural number. At the frontier of our understanding lies a widely believed conjecture asserting that $MAJORITY$ does not belong to $ACC^0$.
  A few years ago, Bhrushundi, Hosseini, Lovett and Rao (ITCS 2019) introduced torus polynomial approximations as an approach towards this conjecture. Torus polynomials approximate Boolean functions when the fractional part of their value on Boolean points is close to half the value of the function. They reduced the conjecture that $MAJORITY \notin ACC^0$ to a conjecture concerning the non-existence of low degree torus polynomials that approximate $MAJORITY$.
  We reduce the non-existence problem further, to a statement about finding feasible solutions for an infinite family of linear programs. The main advantage of this statement is that it allows for incremental progress, which means finding feasible solutions for successively larger collections of these programs. As an immediate first step, we find feasible solutions for a large class of these linear programs, leaving only a finite set for further consideration. Our method is inspired by the method of dual polynomials, which is used to study the approximate degree of Boolean functions. Using our method, we also propose a way to progress further.
  We prove several additional key results with the same method, including lower bounds for approximating the $AND$ function, lower bounds when the approximating polynomial is symmetric, showcasing the power of our machinery.

</details>
